<Review>So we went for lunch and the flavor wasn't bad and the prices were decent. However, the lady taking our order didn't even bother telling us about the daily specials she just asked if we wanted free miso soup. We didn't even see the specials until after we paid because the sign was on the long end past the counter, past the register. What equally upset me was we did order something that was on the special menu, but since we were looking up at the menu and not directly at the hidden specials sign, she charged us full price. When we finally walked past the specials sign and noticed what we ordered was on special, she looked right at us. She didn't offer to substitute something for us overpaying or offer to give us the difference. We just nodded our heads and sat down.

As you can see from my pictures the salmon roll was odd. They put cooked salmon inside a salmon sushi roll...lol. it was strange enough that my 3 kids winced at it. They are used to seeing it uncooked. The flavor wasn't bad, but it wasn't great. I will not order it again thats for sure.

The ginger beef dish was really good and we loved the to go containers they serve their food in. It's super convenient!!!

This place is decent for cheap college students who can't afford actual good sushi or higher end Japanese restaurants.  Its like....a Japanese fast food place, all about the amount of people coming in and not about the quality. But for a quick bite, fairly inexpensive, and not expecting high standards, this place is will do.</Review>< date>

Wanted to try a different crepe in this area and choose this one for the cute presentation. Ordered a custom crepe:

Expresso ice cream with chocolate sauce, pudding, custard and whipped cream. Original crepe batter (optional green tea)

Every ingredient was delicious. It had a large amount of whipped cream but it helped balance out the sweetness of the ice cream. The chocolate sauce had small bits of chocolate which greatly helped the texture of the crepe since we ordered all soft ingredients.

There's only 3 tables in the storefront but there are plenty of seats throughout the mall.

Tip: You always need whipped cream. I thank the worker for asking us. CASH ONLY<//review>

<review>I only came here to pay $8 a crepe because I love novelty food, anything cute, sugar, and well, crepes and ice cream. TBH, I feel like I could stick a couple of colored corn chips and a marshmallow on a scoop of ice cream and call it a bear. Or a dog. Or elephant...

I like the crepe part which was soft and chewy, and the ice cream (I chose vanilla) was really good too. I tired the green and it tasted natural and not artificial.

<Rate>4<//Rate>< review>
Sophie's Crepes usually has too long of a wait, so this place another great option. The wait here is never too bad, even if there's a line. Unlike Sophie's Crepes, the crepes at Belly Good are softer. There's also a lot of options for making custom crepes, but their premade ones are extremely delicious as well! They're known for their "happy face" crepes--which essentially means they'll make some kind of adorable sculpture out of the ice cream on your crepe. Always puts a smile to my face. :)< /review>

<rate>4< /rate>< text>
Sooo cute. I think the crepes are good (not mind-blowing) but it's fun getting a crepe with a cute animal face on it. I got a strawberry cheesecake ice cream with whipped cream and a red bean add-on. The red bean was a bad idea and didn't meld.

The crepe itself is soft and chewy, which I really liked but I understand that others prefer a crispy crepe. It held up well, even after eating for a while - instead of getting my hands very sticky.

All in all, the face was adorable and made me smile but I kind of wish I had gotten the face-less banana and cream cheese crepe that they had on the menu. Next time!< /text>

<UserId.>110006480612793104456<//UserId.><Name>Steven Vong<//Name><date>1430416799991</date><rating>4<//rating>< review>
Come here if you want to instagram/snapchat/(add other social media) a picture of an adorable animal-shaped ice cream crepe. For a little over $5, you get a crepe with ice cream flavor + sauce of your choice adorned with other toppings to create an overly-cute animal face.

I got a green tea bear with marshmallow snout and fruit loop ears, and paired my ice cream with honey (one of my favorite combos is gt + honey). The crepe was warm, fresh and delicious, and all of the ingredients generally balanced well to make a not overly-sweet dessert. Other toppings such as fruit, having a green tea flavor batter, and sweets will run you a little extra, but they have tons of customization options. My simple crepe was still quite solid, and recommended as a photo-op and snack while taking a break from shopping in Japantown.< /review>

I had always been intrigued by the idea of a stretch therapy session. I read the reviews here and was skeptical because people talked about being cured of pain. I thought might as well just try and see. Won't hurt to give it a shot.

My appointment with Derrick was great. He explained everything and made sure pressure was good. After I felt great but was wondering if the relief from my chronic low back pain would last. I've had massages before and the relief only lasts a day or two then pain comes back.

A week later I still felt AMAZING and the best I had felt in years. Not exaggerating when I say this place worked wonders on me. I'm a wedding photographer and had so much pain by hour 3-4 and now that I visit twice a month, I can get through hour 8 with almost no pain. It's incredible. I thought I'd always be in pain but no more

I highly recommend stretch u to anybody who has tried other methods of pain relief, especially pain of unknown origin. It works wonders for me and I will keep going in for the foreseeable future!!</review>

< text>
I was coming to the studio one morning from the city and my left front tire started to go.

George Oren Tire was able to fit me in within the second wave of business and I had to wait less time than I would at another tire service (Except for Boris - but that is another story) and the same amount of time I would wait at at oil change service.  Pretty performing.

Plus, the manager was able to evaluate and recommend quickly and cost effectively.  My service began shortly thereafter following a pleasant conversation with another customer who bragged she'd been bringing all her vehicles there forever.

But before I let the sparkle get the dazzle in my eyes, I waited to see how things went.  My tire needed plugging and they found another that needed plugging that I didn't even know about while performing inspection.

The manager told me that because he had already quoted me one price for the first plug, he wasn't going to charge me for the second one.  He said he was not a pump and dumper, and I laughed with him.

Things went great and he did a free rotation included.  It has been running well since, but my experience working in service stations taught me not to rely on plugged tires so much as new ones, and Oren management advised rightly so while simultaneously estimating two good new tires for the maintenance of my vehicle.

About three weeks later when I was looking for the money to grab two new tires where the plugged ones were running, I got a 20% discount coupon on service which would have brought me to less than 100 dollars each for the new tires installed.

Unfortunately, I couldn't catch that wave, but I bet he will honor the offer if I brings in the June expiring coupon sometime this July.

Even if he doesn't I recommend their service to everyone and rate highest my own experience with George Oren Tire Specialist.

The LC

UPDATE: 7/14/2018:

Glad to hear my coupon is still valid and I look forward to conducting business soon.

The LC< /text>

< Date>

< Text>
Location has always been clean and has also been remodeled recently to provide a nicer space to work and collaborate. This location is near businesses and the freeway so customers tend to come in waves with a lot of people whom are always in a hurry. There is a drive through. Sometimes the drive through line is long so I park and go inside to order...however honestly the staff is pretty efficient so the times I've waited in the drive through lines have been fast anyway. Staff is very friendly, very efficient, and make tasty beverages quickly.

This location tends to cater to busy people on the go, so the environment is a bit less relaxed than other Starbucks locations because of consumer needs and demands. I find that all this considered, the management and staff at this location does an amazing job fulfilling orders efficiently.</Text>
